Shen Bao Local Supplement

Theory

Where is Evolution? 219

— Buddha

Yesterday, I talked about a "circular evolution," which reminded me of our country's evolution.

The Republic of China is more evolved than the Qing Dynasty, and the post-Republic of China is more evolved than the pre-Republic of China. Not only do we Chinese admit this, but even a few "gibberish-speaking" foreign gentlemen would probably admit it.

But when I look back and think about it, where is the evolution? Several foreign PhDs丨or maybe you don't need to go abroad, as long as you enter high school, or just cross the threshold of the university hall丨the clothes you wear must be foreign-made Western clothes, and the things used at home, if you step into a noble family, the room is decorated with strange and bizarre things, mostly foreign goods.

Even in this war, the enemy has airplanes, cannons, warships, and tanks, all fully equipped. And us? We only have a few new-style machine guns, rifles, etc., which are also bought with money from other countries. I ask, where is our country's evolution?

We have it! We have evolved! We have certainly evolved! We are busy dancing, busy watching movies, busy with public socializing, busy with mixed bathing for men and women, busy with free marriage and free divorce, especially modern girls, with strange clothes and ever-changing styles, and everything else has evolved in line with the trend of the times.

Besides that, where is the evolution?

Literature

Lamenting the Battlefield Today 220

— Zheng Zelin

Unbearable to look back at my homeland, only wild grass remains amidst the dark, broken wormwood. The flames of war wound my heart as deer are chased. The desolate people drink bitterness, scattered like startled swans. The phosphorus congeals in patches, the mounds still green. The afterglow reflects the desolate ramparts, about to turn red. Du Fu was weary on the Shu Road in the past. Now, seeing this, I should shed tears like him.

Feeling the Times 221

— Zhu Yunzong

The beautiful rivers and mountains are a lamentable decline, the former capital full of thorns. The Huangxie Dock is empty with only the moon. The banks of the Heilong River are already without spring. Eight thousand children have become weeping blood. Hundreds of thousands of refugees have turned into ashes. I want to wield my sword and ask with a sideways glance, who are the people who bring disaster to the country?

Science

Simple and Easy Small Industries 222

— Naizheng

Recently, I tried to manufacture several daily necessities and all were successful. Now, I dare not keep them secret, so I first select the easiest to manufacture, and those that are most likely to succeed, and write them below:

Prussian Blue Printing Water

Twelve parts distilled water, four parts glycerin, three parts alcohol, dozens of drops of acetic acid. Combine the above four ingredients, stir evenly with chopsticks, then add one part of extremely pure Prussian blue powder and mix well. It can be stored in a glass bottle. The most important thing to note is that the purer the chemicals used, the better the product will be. Acetic acid and Prussian blue powder must be selected from the best quality.

Peppermint Lozenges

Five ounces of camphor, half an ounce of menthol. Place them together in a coarse bowl and heat over a fire. After a while, the two substances will melt and mix. Then pour them into a mold and press them into shape. They are more effective than the peppermint lozenges sold on the market, because more menthol is used in this formula. Western pharmaceutical factories generally use this formula to make peppermint lozenges, but the market is full of Japanese goods, which sell widely because of their low price. However, they do not use much menthol. Therefore, because the raw materials are very expensive, Japanese goods are ultimately not good.

Glue

One hundred parts yellow gelatin (available in Chinese pharmacies, cheap, one copper coin can buy a stick), one hundred parts water, forty parts alcohol, ten parts vinegar, one part alum (pure). First, place the yellow gelatin and water in a bowl, steam until dissolved, and mix well. Then add the other ingredients.

Learning to Write

Test Questions 223

— Qiqi

The other day, this publication had an article "The Level of University Students," which included "Several Answers from Transfer Students from a Certain University." It sounded very real, but a certain university would never ask "Who is Doihara?" or ask about Song Ziwen or Cai Yuanpei in its entrance exams for transfer students. So I think this author is a bit "comedic." Speaking of today's university students, there are indeed many who are unwilling to study hard, watching movies, dating, and going to dance halls. So yesterday, when our eighteen classmates had a meeting, I took the opportunity to present ten test questions as a fun activity and asked them to write down the answers on paper. The papers were all handed in within twenty minutes. They wrote very clearly, very detailed, and very interesting. Now I have revised and copied them down to introduce them to readers.

1. What are the five major theaters?

Answer: Nanjing, Xinguang, Guotai, Carlton, Guanglu.

2. What are the three major parks?

Answer: Zhaofeng Park, Hongkou Park, French Park.

3. The cause of Miss ×'s heartbreak.

Answer: The biggest reason is that her lover already loves someone else. The cause was on August 4, 1931, when Miss × was walking in the campus, eating peanuts, and happened to meet Mr. ×, who refused to give him a few peanuts. So the two started scolding each other. At the time, another couple was trying to reconcile them, but there were bound to be scars in their hearts. On December 17, it happened to be Sunday, at 7:13 pm, the two took a car to the ×× dance hall. At 12:35 am, Mr. × went crazy with joy and accidentally touched a glass with his arm. Coffee and tea spilled on Miss ×'s leather coat, stockings, and shoes. So the two started scolding each other again in the dance hall. From then on, Mr. × fell in love with another girl, and Miss × was heartbroken.

4. Who is the current queen of a certain girls' school?

Answer: ××× Ms. (All eighteen answered correctly).

5. What is the address of the ×× dance hall?

Answer: ××× Road, 1652. (Twelve answered correctly, four could not write the number, two only wrote the road name).

6. What is the purpose of university students living off-campus?

Answer: (1) Freedom. Living off-campus, there is no hateful dormitory supervisor to prohibit us from singing loudly at night, and no other classmates to disturb our sweet love talk during the day. (2) Convenience. Off-campus, you can use electric fans in summer and rent electric stoves in winter, and you can also use electric kettles, etc., which is impossible on-campus. (3) Quiet. Sitting alone to write love letters, no classmates peep through the window, so you can write with peace of mind and not make mistakes, saving hundreds of sheets of stationery every month. There is no such quiet on-campus.

7. What is love-ism?

Answer: Love-ism is the only good medicine to save us university students from boredom, and it must be realized in the shortest possible time.

Answer: Love-ism is saving me-ism. (Seven people wrote this way.)

8. What are the Five Classics?

Answer: Love Classic, Eating Classic, Bible, Clothing Classic, Love Classic. (All eighteen answered correctly.)

9. Who is Qinni Gagno?

Answer: American movie queen.

10. What is Abandoned Woman?

Answer: It is the name of a sound film, starring Norma Shearer. It is very good. I have seen this film six times.

All eighteen papers were answered very well, and all could be scored from 90 to 100 points. It can be seen that university students can pass this type of common sense test.

A Corner of Society

Classmate's Sister-in-law 224

— Fang

One Sunday afternoon, I visited my classmate, Ms. ×, and while we were chatting, she remembered something that I will write down below.

She said to me, "Sister Fang, my sister-in-law, was married to Mr. ×× of the Ministry of Education by my aunt last year. Their love was so intense that it could be said to have reached the boiling point. People often called them a perfect couple. Since the September 18th Incident, Mr. ×× has said to my sister-in-law, "Now the country has reached this point, and the government is holding on to the principle of non-resistance, giving the wealthy three northeastern provinces to others without any effort. Alas, with the country like this, what hope is there?"

My sister-in-law said, "Don't sigh here. The last hope of the country is the responsibility of the youth. So, if everyone is like you, not working hard to build strength, how can the country not perish?"

Mr. ×× said, "The reason why I don't serve on the front lines, sacrificing for the country and the nation, is that I can't forget you and a happy family." My sister-in-law said, "A man of great ambition should be in all directions. What can be missed by a woman and a family, shirking responsibility?" Their passionate words seemed to still be in my mind.

Unfortunately, the January 28th Incident happened again. Mr. ×× was in Beijing researching his affairs. My sister-in-law did not hear the true news in advance, so she did not move to the concession. That night, she was awakened from her warm and sweet dream by the ruthless gunfire. She hurriedly fled to a remote place with Granny Li from next door. After many detours and the terror of the war, she was separated from Granny Li. Later, it was unknown whether she was buried by artillery fire or killed by enemy soldiers.

Afterwards, I told Mr. ×× what Granny Li said, but I knew that he was not sad at all when he heard the news. At that time, my heart was filled with doubts. I thought, their love was so intense, how could he not be sad at all now? Later, I learned that after he went to Beijing, he met a girlfriend and went in and out of dance halls, movie theaters, fancy restaurants, and other happy places every day. How could he still remember his former wife?

Alas, society now is so dark. If we women are not careful, we will fall into a deep pit. Love and marriage are all cheating women, like fish greedy for a small bait and getting hooked. At this time, it is too late to repent. Women! Hurry up and go on the bright path.

You

Essays in the Popular Style 226

— Nai Chang

After reading Buddhist Gentleman's "Essays in the Official Style," I thought of studying "Essays in the Popular Style." In an era of separation between the government and the people, each has its own style of writing.

The lingering poison of the eight-legged essay still exists today. Phrases like "Heaven sends disaster to China, foreign insults frequently arise..." are recited fluently by committee members and secretaries, who can produce such writings effortlessly. Whenever there is a slight change within the country, this type of rhetoric takes center stage. Telegrams and declarations are issued like a string of pearls, creating a great commotion.

The most amusing and incomprehensible thing is that, lacking funds to send telegrams, they advocate for so-called fashionable "express mail instead of telegram," which also becomes very popular.

This is a popular style essay influenced by officialdom.

(II)

Down with [Censored]

All circles unite to [Censored]

Support [Censored]

These are familiar and actively used formulas for our friends in the Republic of China. Even youngsters who haven't lost their baby teeth can manipulate a pen and fill in the "down with [Censored]" formula. Papers with phrases like "Heaven is high, Earth is wide, my family has a little boy..." often appear in the streets and alleys. These are probably sworn brothers of the "down with [Censored]" formulas, suitable for self-cultivation and managing the family.

The new generation of youth has grand visions and likes essays on governing the country and pacifying the world. The older generation has limited vision and likes essays on self-cultivation and managing the family. In short, these are all essays in the popular style.

(III)

"When the mind is unsettled, consult divination" is truly a matter of course.

When Wang San's job application fails, Li Si's illness shows no improvement, and Zhao Wu wants to take a concubine, these are the most delightful opportunities for Layman [Censored] and Taoist [Censored], and also the reason why the yellow-faced women in Buddhist temples wear joyful smiles.

"Good luck at [number] years old, check and deduct any arrears..."

"[Year] fleeting fortune, [deity] in charge..."

"The [number] spirit oracle stick. Upper-middle, middle-lower, upper-upper great auspiciousness."

This kind of cliché occupies an extremely large position in Chinese society and is also one of the essays in the popular style.

(IV)

"Refugee, [number] years old, family of five, fled in panic from the war zone..."

One can often see such refugees along Avenue Edward VII. Chalk is used to write formulaic essays on the ground, invariably saying "lonely and helpless..." unable to make a living... a family of five, old and young, relies entirely on the help of benevolent people..." So says person A, and so says person B. I don't understand why refugees fleeing the war zone are always families of five. Never four, and never six.

This is the fourth type of essay in the popular style.

(V)

Wang Jixu starves himself to save the nation, Zhang Xuewen commits suicide out of concern for the country. We, the descendants of the Yellow Emperor, are truly capable of sacrifice, and incidents of martyrdom are common.

"Unable to bear to live selfishly in the face of national crisis... I wish my compatriots to unite and rise up to save the country" are excerpts from the posthumous writings of those who commit suicide or die for the nation.

The municipal government lacks funds and offers discounts on salaries, because "the national crisis is at hand." Person A and person B die for love, leaving a will saying "the national crisis is at hand." Even when an old couple quarrels, and one dies of anger, it can be said "the national crisis is at hand."

This is also one of the essays in the popular style.

(VI)

"Dearest sister..." How sickening!

If you are fortunate enough to be a postal inspector, you will surely be able to read these gaudy and sickening words all day long. Perhaps Minister Chen advocates increasing postal rates, and this is one of the self-evident reasons.

Writing "Dearest..." is the only job of university students in the classroom. Reading "Dearest..." is the only pastime of middle school students in the toilet.

This is the sixth type of essay in the popular style.

The Bread Problem

Shanghai Life 227

— Yi Ping

(I) Dancers and Night Soil Collectors

Shanghai is spinning non-stop, with all kinds of people struggling to survive in all kinds of environments. Its superficial prosperity prevents tourists who first arrive on the Huangpu River from seeing the curses and sobs behind the scenes. Dancers and night soil collectors seek survival in completely different Shanghai environments. The former ends the Shanghai night, while the latter begins the Shanghai morning. In "Shanghai Life," I especially start with them to express the idea that Shanghai is spinning non-stop.

Under the ghastly green light, dancers spin under people's fetishistic psychology. They flaunt their coquettish eyes and trembling hips... satisfying the dance patrons who pay four dimes each time. The dance patrons' fetishistic psychology is further fueled by champagne - in other words, the temptation of money - to achieve a further purpose: to immerse themselves in a life of alcohol and lust with their flesh and blood in order to survive. They only end their previous day's life and get rest every early morning. When they are spewed out of the big buildings like demons, the night soil collectors also begin their day's work with their labor. They lack good nutrition and adequate sleep, and they come out from pigsty-like homes every day to work, then move their tired bodies back into the pigsties. Dancers, night soil collectors, and all human beings are struggling to survive in the spinning Shanghai life.

(II) Mr. Editor

Mr. Editor Wu Jin stepped into the writing room, looked at the piles of letters on the table, first squeezed his eyebrows and shook his head. The tea boy diligently brought him a plate of egg fried rice. He filled his stomach, lit a cigarette, reluctantly published the manuscripts, and prepared to go home early (his wife was sick), but the typesetter ran over and said that there were still a dozen lines of manuscript missing. He flipped through the incoming manuscripts, but none of them were suitable. He sat down and racked his brains, because he was focused on his wife at home, and he wrote a few lines of filler that were incoherent. He looked at the clock - twelve o'clock, still a few minutes short. A rickshaw pulled over on the desolate road, and you could clearly hear the sound of the rickshaw puller's feet hitting the asphalt road. Suddenly, a rush of sound came from behind. Wu Jin

Page 16

couldn't help but be startled, thinking that the "skinning pig" gentleman had come to visit. He reluctantly calmed down, only to find that it was also a rickshaw chasing from behind, with a dancer with hedgehog-like hair sitting on it. Mr. Wu Jin secretly found it funny.

Walking into the bedroom, he saw his wife's pale face, her lips moving as if to say why he was so late. He picked up the thermos, which was empty. Returning at midnight and unable to get a cup of warm tea, Mr. Wu Jin wrote in his diary "...This hard editing job, I am determined to resign from tomorrow," and he wrote a letter of resignation.

Tomorrow came like today, and Mr. Wu Jin entered his writing room in the same way.

End

Selling Long Ingots 228

"Do you want long ingots! Selling long ingots!" A woman in rural attire called out in the alleys shrouded in the night.

The black lacquered doors of each house immediately opened, some calling to buy, others shouting to come over. You ten coppers, he eight coppers, and in no time, strings of paper ingots were sold out. The woman, carrying a rich harvest, left with a victorious smile, swaying.

Each family that bought long ingots immediately burned them outside the door. The paper ashes danced, fluttering like butterflies. Once the paper butterflies had flown away, the doors of each house slammed shut with a bang.

Everyone says that burning these twice a month, on the first and fifteenth days, can get the blessing of heaven, eliminate disasters and bring blessings, and the cost is only a few coppers, which is a great bargain. And those who sell long ingots live off this kind of psychology.

Hearing the sound of long ingots means knowing that it is already the first and fifteenth days. Knowing that it is already the first and fifteenth days of the long-forgotten lunar calendar. Therefore, the seller of long ingots is the reporter of the abandoned calendar, the supporter of the abandoned calendar, and the extent of superstition among Shanghai people is also evident.

Electric News

The giant film "Charlie Chan's Chance," which combines mystery and love in a Chali Chan case, is bizarre, amazing. The film tells the story of a Scottish detective chief who was killed. The deceased had been investigating a murderer and was brutally killed as soon as he obtained a clue. Famous detectives from England and New York cooperated to investigate this double homicide, but not only could they not find any clues, but they also fell into a fog and were helpless. The great Chinese detective Charlie Chan happened to be in New York investigating the use of punishment in police courts. He was invited to investigate the case. Mr. Chen adopted a unique approach, using his calm and calm mind to capture the murderer, and also cleared a pair of young men and women and four others who were suspected by the police of being heavily suspected. The film is so mysterious and bizarre, and Charlie Chan's dissection skills are breathtaking. The film has recently been released at the Nanjing Grand Theater. Those who love to watch detective novels and films should watch it first.

It is expected that the materials used will be more refined than before.

It has been opened a few days ago. The departments include fashion underwear, outerwear, silk and satin, suits, and western hats. In a few days, many ladies from all walks of life came to visit enthusiastically.

"Fly-Er-Sheng Spray" sprays everywhere, and bedbugs disappear. "Earth Brand Mosquito Repellent Incense" lights a disc and all mosquitoes and flies are wiped out. "Wuzhou Cologne" is fragrant and refreshing, a must-have for bathing. As summer approaches, all products are already on the market. Wholesale buyers are endless. The main company on the Fourth Road of this port, the Hougong Bridge, Xiaodongmen, and the Penglai Market, all Wuzhou branches, and retail business are very prosperous.

Civil Rulings One Item: Luo Jingci: Your petition for enforcement is granted. After reviewing the petition, the case is under appeal, so the enforcement request should be delayed. This is the ruling. ▲ Chen Zelin and others' petition for issuing a certificate for managing the estate. After reviewing the petition, the court's previous ruling ordered the petitioners to publish the draft announcement in the newspaper for five consecutive days. After twenty days, they should submit the newspaper clippings for verification. Now, only the April 9th newspaper clippings have been submitted. It is impossible to determine whether the petitioners complied with the previous ruling to publish the announcement in the newspaper for five consecutive days. The request for issuing the certificate should be processed after the newspaper clippings have been submitted for review. This is the ruling. ▲ One Item: Shi Lei's petition for exemption from enforcement. After reviewing the petition, the debtor Gao Kezhi's car was previously seized. Now, it is stated that the debtor has obtained the petitioner's consent to repay in installments after his financial situation improves, and he requests exemption from enforcement. This should be approved. Order that officials be dispatched to unseal the car on a scheduled date. This is the ruling. ▲ One Item: Dahua Auction Company's request to remove the estimated value of light bulbs. After reviewing the submission, in the case of Zhi Da Printing Materials Bureau, etc., versus Zhang Jianqiu for debt enforcement, the company has legally conducted a fair appraisal. The appraised value listed should be the standard for the auction. The claim that a batch of unexamined light bulbs were appraised at a price of fifty-nine yuan is harmful to the interests of both parties. Furthermore, it is questionable why the prices were rashly assessed without inspection at the time of appraisal. Therefore, the request is difficult to approve. This is the ruling. ▲ One Item: Hu Shusheng's request for issuing a certificate for managing the estate. After reviewing the petition, the certificate for managing the estate is approved. Order that you come to the court at 2:00 PM on the 20th of this month to collect the certificate and file the newspaper. This is the ruling. ▲ One Item: Zhu Guangfu versus Zhu Xiangsheng for rent arrears and provisional attachment. Request for refunding the guarantee deposit. After reviewing the petition, the request for refunding the guarantee deposit of one hundred yuan is approved. Order that the petitioner come to the court at 9:00 AM on the 23rd of this month to collect the deposit. This is the ruling. ▲ One Item: Di Baike versus Fan Youcheng for rent arrears and provisional attachment. Agent Yu Dazhong's request for refunding the guarantee deposit. After reviewing the petition, the case has been withdrawn. The previous guarantee deposit of one hundred yuan is approved for refund. Order that you come to the court at 9:00 AM on the 23rd of this month to collect the deposit. This is the ruling. (May 19th)

Shanghai Local Court 231

Criminal Judgments

Gu Fen Theft Case (Main Text): Gu Fen, taking advantage of the victim's distress, committed theft and is sentenced to six months imprisonment. The number of days of detention shall be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day.

Huo Dongshan and Others Indecent Assault Case (Main Text): Huo Dongshan, with the joint intention of profit, enticed a man under the age of twenty and is sentenced to one year imprisonment. The number of days of detention shall be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. Li Jiade, for receiving and harboring the enticed person, is sentenced to six months imprisonment. The number of days of detention shall be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day.

Cao Suixiang Opium Case (Main Text): Cao Suixiang, intending to use it for criminal purposes, possessed opium substitutes and is fined sixty yuan. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, it shall be converted to imprisonment at a rate of one yuan for one day. The number of days of detention shall be converted to a fine at a rate of one day for one yuan.

▲Li Liangfu Opium Case (Main Text): Li Liangfu, intending to sell opium, possessed opium and is sentenced to six months imprisonment and fined one thousand two hundred yuan. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, it shall be converted to imprisonment at a rate of three yuan for one day. The number of days of detention shall be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day.

▲Zhang Wusheng Embezzlement Case (Main Text): Zhang Wusheng embezzled items held in the course of his business and is sentenced to eight months imprisonment. The number of days of detention shall be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day.

▲Guan Yunsheng and Others Theft Case (Main Text): Guan Yunsheng stole property belonging to others and is sentenced to two months imprisonment. Wu Xu Shi repeatedly stole property belonging to others and is sentenced to three months imprisonment. The number of days of detention shall be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day.

▲He Shouzheng and Others Robbery, Gambling, and Opium Case (Main Text): Zhang Jinyong's trial is suspended. Zhang Rijin, Wang Xinzhi, and Chen Dalong are found not guilty of robbery. Wang Xinzhi, intending to profit, opened a establishment for others to smoke opium and is sentenced to one year imprisonment. The number of days of detention shall be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. Zhang Rijin, assisting in the intention to profit by providing opium for others to smoke, is sentenced to one year imprisonment. The number of days of detention shall be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. He Shouzheng and Ding Asi are found not guilty of gambling. He Shouzheng is found not guilty of possessing military firearms. He Zheng Shi, for possessing military firearms and ammunition, is sentenced to three months imprisonment. The number of days of detention shall be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day.

▲Ruling: Chen Haishan's Appeal Case Regarding Chen Zhongzhang's Embezzlement (Main Text): This appeal is rejected.

▲Li Hongyong Embezzlement Case (Main Text): Li Hongyong, intending to illegally possess it for himself, repeatedly embezzled property belonging to others that he held in the course of his business and is sentenced to six months imprisonment. Li Hongyong shall return 869.87 silver dollars to Juyuan Yongji Sock Factory.

▲Zhao Wangshan and Others Theft Case (Main Text): Zhao Yushan, Xu Shunlin, Shen Heshang, Chen Jinguan, Li Chang, and Zhao Jinming, as a group, are each sentenced to six months imprisonment for theft. The number of days of detention shall be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. Yu Zijun stole property belonging to others and is sentenced to two months imprisonment. For smoking opium, he is sentenced to two months imprisonment. The sentence to be executed is three months imprisonment. The number of days of detention shall be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day.

▲Zong Along and Others Illegal Detention Case (Main Text): Zong Along, Wang Xingsheng, and Qiu Mingyou, jointly using violence and coercion to force others to do what they are not obligated to do, are each fined fifteen yuan. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, it shall be converted to imprisonment at a rate of one yuan for one day. The number of days of detention shall be converted to a fine at a rate of one day for one yuan.

▲Xie Hechuang Injury Case (Main Text): This public prosecution is not accepted.

▲Pan Renqing Embezzlement Case (Main Text): Pan Renqing, intending to illegally possess it for himself, embezzled property belonging to others that he held and is sentenced to thirty days of detention. The number of days of detention shall be converted to detention at a rate of two days for one day.

Civil Judgments

Ye Pengyuan and Jiang Chunrong Goods Payment Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff's goods payment of 262.6 silver dollars. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲Zhuang Zhengxin and Dai Jinxian Rental Case (Main Text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff's overdue rent of 250 silver dollars. The lease agreement between the defendant and the plaintiff shall be terminated. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲Yao Shanda and Yang Dequan et al. Debt Appeal Case (Main Text): The original judgment regarding the rejection of the appellant's claim and the litigation costs is reversed. The appellee Yang Dequan shall return to the appellant 308.95 silver dollars for goods. If unable to repay, Huo Ernan shall repay on his behalf. The litigation costs of this appeal and the first instance regarding the disputed part shall be borne by the appellee Yang Dequan.

▲Ma Haiyang Firm and Ling Jiannan Rent Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the overdue rent of 435 silver dollars and the water bill of 18 silver dollars. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

▲Xi Changlin and Huang Fuqing Mortgage Appeal Case (Main Text): The appeal is rejected. The appeal costs shall be borne by the appellant.

▲Qian Zhengfu and Gu Hongqiao et al. Ownership Confirmation Appeal Case (Main Text): The appeal is rejected. The appeal costs shall be borne by the appellant.

▲He Xing Real Estate Company and Gu Tai et al. Rental Case (Main Text): The defendant Chai Zhenggao shall repay the plaintiff's rent of 136 silver dollars. Lu Jiafu and Chen Cunyu shall each repay the plaintiff's rent of 124 silver dollars and shall each vacate the premises. The plaintiff's request for provisional execution is rejected.

▲Wu Deling and Cao Axiang et al. Rent and Compensation Case (Main Text): The defendant Cao Axiang shall repay the plaintiff 50 silver dollars, including 19 silver dollars for rent. If unable to repay, Hu Rensheng shall be responsible for repayment on his behalf. The plaintiff's remaining claims are rejected. The litigation costs, except for one-half of the rejected portion, which shall be borne by the plaintiff, shall be borne by the defendant Cao Axiang in one-half.

▲Li Fusun and Wang Jutang Rice Payment Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff's rice payment of 40.02 silver dollars. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. The first item of this judgment shall be subject to provisional execution by public notification. (The full text is posted at the court's display area.)

Xue Maohua and Zhang Jinbiao et al. Execution Objection Retrial Case: This court has set June 10th at 10:00 AM as the date for public hearing. In addition to directly appointing lawyer Zhou Cheng as the special agent for the appellant Zhang Liansheng, the defendant is instructed to appear in court on time for debate and not delay. This public notification is hereby issued for the appellant Zhang Liansheng to be informed.

▲Shen Ziyi's payment and request for a two-installment extension for the remaining payment is noted. The debt payment to the case is retained. After notifying the creditor to collect, the remaining installments shall be paid on time. Any delays will result in strict pursuit. This ruling.

▲Fang Gongshi's petition for execution is noted. Upon review, the case file has not yet been returned, so the request will be postponed for discussion. This ruling.

One case: Liu Bin's petition for execution is noted. The case has been appealed, so the request will be postponed for discussion. This ruling.

▲One case: Tao Bairong's petition for strict execution is noted. Await the transfer of the case for strict pursuit. This ruling.

▲One case: Zhang Hongru et al.'s petition for execution is noted. Await transfer for pursuit. This ruling.

▲One case: Li Jingfen's petition for execution is noted. Await transfer for pursuit. This ruling.

▲One case: Zhengda Bank's request to collect the auction price is noted. Await the completion of the auction process before transferring it to the Shanghai First Special District Local Court, and then the petitioner can go to collect it.

▲Hengsheng Yongji Bean Firm's petition to declare clearance for record is noted. Declaration of liquidation does not require filing. This ruling.

▲Zhang Changyou et al.'s request to postpone the payment of second-instance litigation costs is noted. The individuals should pay 21 silver dollars for the second-instance litigation costs. A ten-day extension is granted for payment. They must submit the payment on time and submit formal litigation documents to supplement the reasons for the appeal to the court for review. Failure to comply will result in rejection. This ruling.

Criminal Rulings

Wu Zhou Shi's request for temporary postponement of interrogation is noted. This case arises from civil causes and produces criminal consequences. The truth and falsehood of the matter are not clear without questioning. Although the request for postponement complies with the law and has some merit in terms of compassion, it is provisionally approved. This ruling.

▲Gu Jiusheng's subsequent request for acceptance and investigation is noted. Since the defendant resides on Avenue Edward VII, it is appropriate for the Special District Court to handle it. This is reiterated for compliance. This ruling.

▲Liu Xuewen's filing is noted. If the defendant has indeed committed criminal acts, report them according to the law. The request for filing is noted, but the current criminal procedure law does not explicitly provide for it, so there is no need for further discussion. This ruling.

▲Yang Wenqi sues Chen Getao for causing death by negligence. It is noted that the public prosecution part of the case has been sentenced by the Criminal Court of this court to a fine of 120 yuan for Chen Getao, which has been executed. This is for your information. This ruling.

▲Pei Chenshi requests to interrogate Li Zhengchao. The request is noted. Come to the court for interrogation. This ruling.

▲Gu Xuewen petitions for interrogation. Petition directly to the Haimen County government to send police to escort him back to the case for interrogation and review. This ruling.

▲Cao Luoshi petitions for interrogation and legal action. Come to the court to await interrogation and review. This ruling.

▲Chen Shi Shi withdraws the case. Permission is granted to withdraw the accusation. This ruling.

▲Zhuang Yunsheng withdraws the case. Permission is granted to withdraw the accusation. This ruling. (May 18th)

Weng Chuanxin and Zheng Junsheng et al. Goods Payment Case: This court has set June 17th at 9:00 AM as the date for public hearing. In addition to appointing lawyer Chen Honglai as the agent for the defendant Zheng Junsheng, the defendant is instructed to appear in court on time for debate and not delay. This public notification is hereby issued for the defendant Zheng Junsheng to be informed.

▲Shen Fuzhou and Rong Huanquan Rent Arrears Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff's rent of 12 silver dollars and return 20 rope-making machines and all assets. The litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. To the defendant Rong Huanquan. (May 16th)

Criminal Judgment

Wang Xiuying Sues Yan Rutang for Offenses Against Morality Case (Main Text): This private prosecution is not accepted.

▲Chen One et al. Theft Case (Main Text): Chen San and Chen Xianghai are each sentenced to two months imprisonment for joint theft. The number of days of detention shall be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. Xing Shechuan et al. Injury and Theft Appeal Case (Main Text): The original judgment regarding the injury crime of Xing Xiaochuan, Xing Wenlin, and Zhou Si is revoked. Xing Xiaochuan, Xing Wenlin, and Zhou Si are all found not guilty. The appeals of the appellants Zhu Wei and Wei Wen are all rejected.

Bill Payment Case (Main Text): The plaintiff's lawsuit is rejected. This case is approved to be transferred to the Shanghai First Special District Local Court for trial.
